facility:

There is a small zoo and children's entertainment facilities in the yard on the first floor, which is also considered a parent-child concept.
health:
The standards of the InterContinental Hotel are relatively reliable. It is clean inside and out, the rooms are cleaned well, and the yard is tidy and suitable for walking.
environment:
It is right on the edge of Xiayang Lake. The rooms on the west side have side lake views, and the balcony of the front lake view room is also on the side, so I think the concept of lake view room is not very accurate. The view throughout the hotel is still very good.
Serve:
It's pretty average, nothing special. The cleaning lady is quite enthusiastic. It's convenient to get some water, slippers, and toothbrushes.
Generally speaking, the price-performance ratio of the price of around 500 yuan including two breakfasts is very high, but the decoration style is a bit old. I feel it is good to live casually in the suburbs.

Environment: The hotel occupies a large area with sufficient parking spaces. The surrounding Qingpu Museum, library, Xiayang Lake, commercial center, etc. are all available. Just walking around can fully meet all the needs of travel.

For a hotel that has been in business for more than ten years, after the baptism of the epidemic, it is really rare to maintain a consistent service quality. I hope it will continue to be maintained, and I will definitely come back when I have the opportunity in the future!
